<img src=\"//cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0075/8682/t/64/assets/care.png?14092113312788012902\" alt=\"\">\n                <h1>Care Instructions</h1>\n                <p class=\"lead\">Our leather, wool and canvas can be softly cleaned with lukewarm water and a mild soap. Keep them away from makeup, food, or any other oil based products which can stain. All liquid stains should be dealt with quickly, and blotted gently with a clean, dry cloth. Don't forget, leather is a skin, and should be cared for in a similar way to your own.</p>\n            </div>\n            <div class=\"block middle\">\n                <div class=\"third\"><p><span>1</span> Don't keep your HARDGRAFT in the rain for long periods of time (keep it under your umbrella). If the product becomes wet wipe away excess moisture and then leave to dry naturally in room temperature. Do not attempt to dry with a direct heat source. </p></div>\n                <div class=\"third mid\"><p><span>2</span> Try to avoid the leather coming in contact with light coloured clothes and vice versa: some clothes (especially denim) lose colour and might rub off onto your HARDGRAFT. Avoid the contact or embrace the developing patina. Your choice. </p></div>\n                <div class=\"third\"><p><span>3</span> If in doubt or you are experiencing some pretty bad staining (yep, you should have closed the fountain pen before you threw it into the bag) go to a special leather cleaning expert. They are still around and can do magic!</p></div>\n            </div>\n            <div class=\"block\">\n                <div class=\"break\"><p>To keep the leather on your product looking its best you can apply natural leather wax, balm or oil. They all have a different effect so please apply on a small corner first. Ask a specialist in your area to recommend the best product to use. The leather tends to go darker if you treat it and does not need to be treated very often.</p></div>\n                <div><p>As our leather is not synthetically treated there is a slim chance that the tannins from the leather could transfer to your clothing the same way that the dye from your jeans can transfer to your HARDGRAFT product. Please consult your local specialist who will be able to advise you on the best way to colour fast your product.</p></div>\n                <div><p>We choose and balance the materials very thoughtfully, the leather is strong and rich, the wool is dense and soft and the canvas rugged and can take quite a bit of beating... and don't get us started on our colours which have a fascinating life of their own! </p></div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n</div>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n           <div id=\"product-grid\">\n  \t  \n\t\t \n\t\t\n  <div class=\"section clearfix\" style=\"display: none;\">\n      <div class=\"paginate\" style=\"display: none;\">\n        \n        \n        <span class=\"current page\"><a href=\"/?page=1\">1</a></span>\n        \n        <span class=\" page\"><a href=\"/?page=2\">2</a></span>\n        \n      </div>\n  </div>\n\n\n\t\n<!--    <h1>Full Range</h1> -->\n<!--    <h2 class=\"intro\">\n     <p>...and voilà!
